> この記事は[人為的な要因による死者数一覧](https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/人為的な要因による死者数一覧)から翻訳されています。


以下は[世界史における](../Page/世界の歴史.md "wikilink")**人為的な要因による死者数一覧**である。一覧では、出来事の名前、場所、それぞれの出来事の開始と終了の時期についても述べている。いくつかの出来事については、そのカテゴリーが一つ以上になる場合もある。また、いくつかの出来事では、他の出来事と重なっている場合もあり、小さな出来事における死者数がさらに大きな出来事の中で発生した一部であることもある。

死者数はほとんどの場合、多くの不確実な部分がある。表では、低い推定値と高い推定値の[相乗平均の順に並べてある](../Page/幾何平均.md "wikilink")。例えば、低い推定値が500人、高い推定値が2000人であったとき\(\sqrt{500 \cdot 2000} = 1000\)となる.

## 高い推定値による死者数が10万人以上となる戦争・武力衝突

*ここでは、高い推定値による死者数が10万人以上となる全ての戦争について一覧を載せる。これには軍人と民間人の両方の死者数が含まれる。直接、戦争によって死亡しただけでなく、それによって引き起こされた[戦闘](../Page/戦闘.md "wikilink")、[病気](../Page/病気.md "wikilink")、[飢餓](../Page/飢餓.md "wikilink")、[虐殺](../Page/虐殺.md "wikilink")、[自殺](../Page/自殺.md "wikilink")、[ジェノサイド](../Page/ジェノサイド.md "wikilink")による死者も含む。*

## 戦争犯罪・虐殺

*ここでは軍事組織によって引き起こされた非戦闘員の死者数の一覧を載せる。特定の民族、宗教、政治的グループをターゲットにしたものに限ることなく、一般市民の生命を軽視した軍事戦略や残虐行為について記述する。*

<table>
<thead>
<tr class="header">
<th><p>出来事</p></th>
<th><p>data-sort-type="number" | 低い推定</p></th>
<th><p>style="width:7%;" data-sort-type="number" | 高い推定</p></th>
<th><p>data-sort-type="number" | 相乗平均</p></th>
<th><p>場所</p></th>
<th><p>開始</p></th>
<th><p>style="width:5%;" data-sort-="" type="number" | 終了</p></th>
<th><p>期間</p></th>
<th><p>style="width:50%;" data-sort-="" type="number" | 備考</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr class="odd">
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/第二次世界大戦" title="wikilink">第二次世界大戦</a>中の戦争犯罪</p></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td><p>Worldwide</p></td>
<td><p>1939</p></td>
<td><p>1945</p></td>
<td><p>6 years</p></td>
<td><p>See also: <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/World_War_II_casualties" title="wikilink">World War II casualties</a>.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="even">
<td><p><a href="../Page/日本の戦争犯罪.md" title="wikilink">日本の戦争犯罪</a></p></td>
<td><p>(lowest estimate to include soldier deaths, famine or disease caused by Japanese imperialism)[63]</p></td>
<td><p>+[64]</p></td>
<td></td>
<td><p>In and around East and South East <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Asia" title="wikilink">Asia</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oceania" title="wikilink">Oceania</a> and the Pacific</p></td>
<td><p>1931</p></td>
<td><p>1945</p></td>
<td><p>8 years</p></td>
<td><p>Japanese <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/war_crimes" title="wikilink">war crimes</a> occurred in many Asian and Pacific countries during the period of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_militarism" title="wikilink">Japanese imperialism</a>, primarily during the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Second_Sino-Japanese_War" title="wikilink">Second Sino-Japanese War</a> and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/World_War_II" title="wikilink">World War II</a>. If total casualties for these conflicts are assigned exclusively to Japanese aggression the toll could reach some 30 million deaths. These incidents have also been described as an Asian Holocaust[65] and Japanese war atrocities.[66][67][68] Some war crimes were committed by <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/military_personnel" title="wikilink">military personnel</a> from the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Empire_of_Japan" title="wikilink">Empire of Japan</a> in the late 19th century, although most took place during the first part of the <em><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shōwa_period" title="wikilink">Shōwa Era</a></em>, the name given to the reign of Emperor <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hirohito" title="wikilink">Hirohito</a>, until the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Surrender_of_Japan" title="wikilink">surrender</a> of the Empire of Japan, in 1945.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="odd">
<td><p><a href="../Page/三光作戦.md" title="wikilink">三光作戦</a></p></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/China" title="wikilink">China</a></p></td>
<td><p>1940</p></td>
<td><p>1942</p></td>
<td><p>2 years</p></td>
<td><p>In a study published in 1996, historian Mitsuyoshi Himeta claims that the Three Alls Policy, a scorched-earth policy implemented by the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Imperial_Japanese_Army" title="wikilink">Imperial Japanese Army</a> on China, sanctioned by <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emperor_Hirohito" title="wikilink">Emperor Hirohito</a> himself, was both directly and indirectly responsible for the deaths of "more than 2.7 million" Chinese civilians.[69]</p></td>
</tr>

<td><p>1975</p></td>
<td><p>2002</p></td>
<td><p>27 years</p></td>
<td><p>The 27-year war can be divided roughly into three periods of major fighting – 1975–91, 1992–94, and 1998 to 2002 – broken up by fragile periods of peace. By the time the MPLA achieved victory in 2002, more than 500,000 people had died and over one million had been <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/internally_displaced" title="wikilink">internally displaced</a>. The war devastated Angola's infrastructure, and severely damaged the nation's public administration, economic enterprises, and religious institutions.</p></td>

<td><p>War crimes during the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internal_conflict_in_Peru" title="wikilink">Internal conflict in Peru</a></p></td>

<td><p><sup>[see notes]</sup></p></td>

<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peru" title="wikilink">Peru</a></p></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td><p>20 years</p></td>
<td><p>In the late 20th century, the Peruvian government (armed forces and civil <em>rondas</em>) fought against communist terrorists in Peru. The principal actors in the war were the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Communist_Party_of_Peru" title="wikilink">Communist Party of Peru</a> or "Shining Path" and the government of Peru; the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tupac_Amaru_Revolutionary_Movement" title="wikilink">Tupac Amaru Revolutionary Movement</a> was also involved and other paramilitary entities. <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Truth_and_Reconciliation_Commission_(Peru)" title="wikilink">Peru's Truth and Reconciliation Commission</a> reached a figure of approx. 68,784 deaths and disappearances, of which 54% were ascribed to Shining Path, 1.5% to Tupac Amaru and 37% to State officials, who were also responsible for 83% of reported cases of sexual violence, and systematic use of torture. An academic research published in 2019 contests the Commission's methodology, reaching a total figure of approx. 47,849, of which 27,872 were victims of State officials, 18,341 of the Shining Path, and 1,636 by all other actors.[124][125]</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="odd">
<td><p>War crimes during the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sheikh_Said_rebellion" title="wikilink">Sheikh Said rebellion</a></p></td>
<td><p>15,000 20,000[126]</p></td>
<td><p>40,000 250,000[127]</p></td>
<td><p>24,495 70,711</p></td>

<td><p>1925</p></td>
<td><p>1925</p></td>
<td><p>1 month</p></td>
<td><p>The <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sheikh_Said_Rebellion" title="wikilink">Sheikh Said Rebellion</a> was a rebellion to revive the Islamic Caliphate System, and used elements of Kurdish nationalism for recruiting.[128] It was led by <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sheikh_Said" title="wikilink">Sheikh Said</a> and a group of former Ottoman soldiers, known as <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hamidiye_(cavalry)" title="wikilink">Hamidiye soldiers</a>. The rebellion was of two Kurdish groups, the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zaza_people" title="wikilink">Zaza people</a> and the speakers of the related <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kurmanji_dialect" title="wikilink">Kurmanji dialect</a> of Kurdish: it "was led specifically by the Zaza population and received almost full support in the entire Zaza region and some of the neighbouring Kurmanji-dominated regions".[129]</p></td>

<td><p>present</p></td>

<tr class="odd">
<td><p>War Crimes during the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sri_Lankan_Civil_War" title="wikilink">Sri Lankan Civil War</a></p></td>
<td><p>[130]</p></td>
<td><p>[131]</p></td>

<td><p>1983</p></td>

<td><p>26 years</p></td>
<td><p>There are allegations that <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/war_crime" title="wikilink">war crimes</a> were committed by the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sri_Lanka_Armed_Forces" title="wikilink">Sri Lankan military</a> and the rebel <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Liberation_Tigers_of_Tamil_Eelam" title="wikilink">Liberation Tigers of Tamil Eelam</a> (Tamil Tigers) during the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sri_Lankan_Civil_War" title="wikilink">Sri Lankan Civil War</a>, particularly during the final months of the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eelam_War_IV" title="wikilink">Eelam War IV</a> phase in 2009. The alleged war crimes include attacks on civilians and civilian buildings by both sides; executions of combatants and prisoners by both sides; enforced disappearances by the Sri Lankan military and paramilitary groups backed by them; acute shortages of food, medicine, and clean water for civilians trapped in the war zone; and child recruitment by the Tamil Tigers.[132][133] </p></td>

## ジェノサイド・民族浄化・迫害

*ここでは人種、宗教、民族に基づいて行われた大量虐殺（または強制移住によって引き起こされた死亡）について一覧を載せている。*

<td><p><a href="../Page/アメリカ州の先住民族.md" title="wikilink">アメリカ先住民虐殺</a></p></td>

<td><p>1996[158][159][160][161]</p></td>

<td><p>While the overall toll of man made deaths of Amerindians is unknown, there have been a few known events in which many Amerindians perished. Thousands to millions more killed in <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Encomienda" title="wikilink">forced labor</a>, wars and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_Indian_massacres" title="wikilink">massacres</a>; Covers both North and South America Unknown number of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Apache" title="wikilink">Apache</a> killed for bounty</p>
<p>See also: <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_colonization_of_the_Americas" title="wikilink">Spanish colonization of the Americas</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Encomienda_system" title="wikilink">Encomienda system</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mexican_Indian_Wars" title="wikilink">Mexican Indian Wars</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_Indian_massacres" title="wikilink">List of Indian massacres</a></p></td>

<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/ホロコースト" title="wikilink">ホロコースト</a></p></td>
<td><p>[162]</p></td>
<td><p>[163][164]</p></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="wikilink">German</a>-occupied Europe</p></td>
<td><p>1941</p></td>
<td><p>1945</p></td>
<td><p>4 years</p></td>
<td><p>The systematic and bureaucratic genocide of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/History_of_the_Jews_in_Europe" title="wikilink">European Jews</a> by <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="wikilink">Germany</a> and its puppet states.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="even">
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/ホロドモール" title="wikilink">ホロドモール</a></p></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukraine" title="wikilink">Ukraine</a></p></td>
<td><p>1932</p></td>
<td><p>1933</p></td>
<td><p>1 year</p></td>
<td><p>The term "Ukrainian Genocide" usually refers to the man-made famine of 1932 through 1933, called the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Holodomor" title="wikilink">Holodomor</a>, in which the grain of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainians" title="wikilink">Ukrainians</a> was confiscated to the point where they could not survive off the amount of grain they had, and were also restricted from fleeing their villages to find food under threat of execution or deportation into a <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gulag" title="wikilink">Gulag</a> camp. The term also includes the killing of Ukrainian intelligentsia during the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Purge" title="wikilink">Great Purge</a>, especially the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Orthodox_Church" title="wikilink">Orthodox Church</a>.</p>
<p>The main advocate for this view was <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Raphael_Lemkin" title="wikilink">Raphael Lemkin</a>, creator of the word <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/genocide" title="wikilink">genocide</a>.</p>
<p>Data from after the opening of the Soviet archives records deaths at 2.4 to 7.5 million in famine, 300,000 during the purge, and 1,100 from the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Law_of_Spikelets" title="wikilink">Law of Spikelets</a>.</p>
<p>Some scholars dispute that the famine was deliberately engineered by the Soviet government or that it was a genocide.[165][166][167]</p>
<p>– Part of the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soviet_famine_of_1932–33" title="wikilink">Soviet famine of 1932–33</a></p></td>

<td><p><a href="../Page/ルワンダ虐殺.md" title="wikilink">ルワンダ虐殺</a>とブルンジ虐殺</p></td>

<td><p>38 years</p></td>
<td><p>Combined death toll of all <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/genocides" title="wikilink">genocides</a> and other massacres between the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hutus" title="wikilink">Hutus</a> and the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tutsis" title="wikilink">Tutsis</a>. Regarded as the most efficient <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/genocide" title="wikilink">genocide</a> of the 20th century, the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rwandan_genocide" title="wikilink">Rwandan genocide</a> was the disorganized communal mass murder of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tutsi" title="wikilink">Tutsi</a>s, by their rival tribe the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hutu" title="wikilink">Hutu</a> through the Rwandan government and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hutu_Power" title="wikilink">Hutu Power</a> militias such as the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Interahamwe" title="wikilink">Interahamwe</a> and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Impuzamugambi" title="wikilink">Impuzamugambi</a>.</p>
<p>Violence peaked in the hundred days between April 7, 1994 and July 15, 1994, during which time between 500,000 and 1,000,000 people were killed.</p></td>

<td><p>カザフスタンの飢饉</p></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>

<tr class="even">
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/チベット問題" title="wikilink">チベットの占領</a></p></td>
<td><p>[185]</p></td>
<td><p>[186]</p></td>

<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tibet" title="wikilink">Tibet</a></p></td>
<td><p>1950</p></td>
<td><p>present</p></td>
<td><p>68 years</p></td>
<td><p>In 1960, the western-based <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nongovernmental_organization" title="wikilink">nongovernmental</a> <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Commission_of_Jurists" title="wikilink">International Commission of Jurists</a> (ICJ) gave a report titled <em>Tibet and the Chinese People's Republic to the United Nations</em>. The report was prepared by the ICJ's Legal Inquiry Committee, composed of eleven international lawyers from around the world. This report accused the Chinese of the crime of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/genocide" title="wikilink">genocide</a> in Tibet, after nine years of full occupation, six years before the devastation of the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/cultural_revolution" title="wikilink">cultural revolution</a> began. The ICJ also documented accounts of massacres, tortures and killings, bombardment of monasteries, and extermination of whole nomad camps. Declassified Soviet archives provides data that Chinese communists, who received a great assistance in military equipment from the Soviets, broadly used Soviet aircraft for bombing monasteries and other punitive operations in Tibet.[187]</p></td>

<td><p>During the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Congo_War" title="wikilink">First Congo War</a>, Rwanda was able to destroy refugee camps, which the <em>génocidaires</em> had been using as their safe-bases, and forcibly repatriate Tutsi to Rwanda. During this process, Rwandan and aligned forces committed multiple atrocities, mainly against Hutu refugees. The true extent of the abuses is unknown because the AFDL and RPF carefully managed NGO and press access to areas where atrocities were thought to have occurred;[195] however, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Amnesty_International" title="wikilink">Amnesty International</a> claimed as many as 200,000 Rwandese Hutu refugees were massacred by them and the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rwandan_Defence_Forces" title="wikilink">Rwandan Defence Forces</a> and aligned forces.[196] The United Nations similarly documented mass killings of civilians by Rwandan, Ugandan and the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alliance_of_Democratic_Forces_for_the_Liberation_of_Congo" title="wikilink">ADFL</a> soldiers in the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/DRC_Mapping_Exercise_Report" title="wikilink">DRC Mapping Exercise Report</a>.</p></td>

<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iraq" title="wikilink">Iraq</a></p></td>
<td><p>1977</p></td>
<td><p>1991</p></td>
<td><p>14 years</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Destruction_of_Kurdish_villages_during_the_Iraqi_Arabization_campaign#Major_population_damaging_events" title="wikilink">87,500 to 388,100 Kurds</a> were killed in the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/destruction_of_Kurdish_villages_during_the_Iraqi_Arabization_campaign" title="wikilink">destruction of Kurdish villages during the Iraqi Arabization campaign</a> including: 2,500[203] to 12,500[204] in the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ba&#39;athist_Arabization_campaigns_in_North_Iraq" title="wikilink">Ba'athist Arabization campaigns in North Iraq</a>, 10,000[205] to 25,000[206][207] were killed during the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Feyli_Kurds_under_Saddam_Hussein" title="wikilink">Feyli Kurds operation</a>, 5,000[208] to 8,000[209] Kurds were disappeared in the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kurdish_rebellion_of_1983" title="wikilink">1983 Barzani killings</a>, 50,000[210] to 100,000[211] (although Kurdish sources have cited a higher figure of 182,000[212]) more Kurds were massacred in the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anfal_genocide" title="wikilink">Anfal genocide</a>, and at least 20,000[213] were killed during the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/1991_Iraqi_uprising" title="wikilink">1991 Iraqi uprising</a> notwithstanding an additional 48,400[214] to 140,600[215] Kurdish refugees that starved to death along the Iranian and Turkish borders.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="odd">
<td><p><a href="../Page/ダルフール.md" title="wikilink">ダルフール</a>虐殺</p></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Darfur" title="wikilink">Darfur</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sudan" title="wikilink">Sudan</a></p></td>
<td><p>2003</p></td>
<td><p>present</p></td>
<td><p>15 years</p></td>
<td><p>The <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/War_in_Darfur" title="wikilink">War in Darfur</a> is a major armed conflict in the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Darfur" title="wikilink">Darfur</a> region of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sudan" title="wikilink">Sudan</a> that began in February 2003 when the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sudan_Liberation_Movement/Army" title="wikilink">Sudan Liberation Movement</a> (SLM) and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Justice_and_Equality_Movement" title="wikilink">Justice and Equality Movement</a> (JEM) rebel groups began fighting the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/government_of_Sudan" title="wikilink">government of Sudan</a>, which they accused of oppressing Darfur's non-<a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arab" title="wikilink">Arab</a> population.[216][217] The government responded to attacks by carrying out a campaign of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/ethnic_cleansing" title="wikilink">ethnic cleansing</a> against Darfur's non-Arabs. This resulted in the deaths of hundreds of thousands of civilians and the indictment of Sudan's president <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Omar_al-Bashir" title="wikilink">Omar al-Bashir</a> for <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/genocide" title="wikilink">genocide</a>, war crimes, and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/crimes_against_humanity" title="wikilink">crimes against humanity</a> by the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Criminal_Court" title="wikilink">International Criminal Court</a>.[218]</p></td>

<tr class="odd">
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ethnic_cleansing_in_the_Bosnian_War" title="wikilink">Ethnic cleansing</a> and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bosnian_genocide" title="wikilink">genocide</a> committed by all sides during the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yugoslav_Wars" title="wikilink">Yugoslav Wars</a></p></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yugoslavia" title="wikilink">Yugoslavia</a> and successor states</p></td>
<td><p>1991</p></td>
<td><p>2001</p></td>
<td><p>10 years</p></td>
<td><p>All civilians killed in the Yugoslav Wars including events such as the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Srebrenica_Massacre" title="wikilink">Srebrenica Massacre</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Žepa#Bosnian_War" title="wikilink">Žepa Massacre</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lašva_Valley_ethnic_cleansing" title="wikilink">Lašva Valley ethnic cleansing</a>, and other atrocities. 69.8% to 82% of civilian victims of the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bosnian_War" title="wikilink">Bosnian War</a> were <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bosniak" title="wikilink">Bosniak</a>. During the War in Croatia, 43.4% of the killed on the Croatian side were civilians.</p>

<td><p>1890</p></td>

<td><p>From the U.S. Bureau of the Census (1894): "The Indian wars under the government of the United States have been more than 40 in number. They have cost the lives of about 19,000 white people, including those killed in individual combats, and the lives of about 30,000 Indians. The actual number of killed and wounded Indians must be very much higher than the given ... Fifty percent additional would be a safe estimate ..." Part of the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Native_American_Genocide" title="wikilink">Genocide of indigenous peoples in the Americas</a>.</p></td>

<td><p>British concentration camps during the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Concentration_camp_(South_Africa)" title="wikilink">Second Boer War</a></p></td>

<td><p>1902</p></td>
<td><p>2 years</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herbert_Kitchener,_1st_Earl_Kitchener" title="wikilink">Lord Kitchener</a> led the British army against the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Boer_Republics" title="wikilink">Boer Republics</a> in the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Second_Boer_War" title="wikilink">Second Boer War</a> in Southern Africa. In an attempt to pacify Boer guerrillas, he targeted their families, and 116,000 Boer women and children were captured and jailed by the British, Within 2 years, 22,074 children died and 4,177 women died due to deliberate neglect by the British. 115,000 black people were separately jailed, of whom 15,000 died in prison camps.[273]</p></td>

<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Fire_of_Smyrna" title="wikilink">Great Fire of Smyrna</a></p></td>

<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Smyrna" title="wikilink">Smyrna</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="wikilink">Ottoman Empire</a></p></td>
<td><p>September 9, 1922</p></td>
<td><p>September 24, 1922</p></td>
<td><p>15 days</p></td>
<td><p>Fires set during attacks on Greeks and Armenians by Turkish mobs and military forces in Smyrna at the end of the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greco-Turkish_War_(1919–1922)" title="wikilink">Greco-Turkish War (1919–1922)</a>. The violence and fires resulted in the destruction of the Greek and Armenian portions of the city and the massacre of their populations.</p>
<p>After the attacks, 30,000 Greek and Armenian men left behind were deported by Turkish forces, many of whom were subsequently killed.</p></td>

A public commission in <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kyrgyzstan" title="wikilink">Kyrgyzstan</a> called the crackdown of 1916 that killed 100,000 to 270,000 Kyrgyzstanis a <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/genocide" title="wikilink">genocide</a>though <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russia" title="wikilink">Russia</a> rejected this characterization.[278]</p>

<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dersim_Massacre" title="wikilink">Dersim Massacre</a></p></td>

<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dersim" title="wikilink">Dersim</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkey" title="wikilink">Turkey</a></p></td>

<td><p>The <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dersim_massacre" title="wikilink">Dersim massacre</a> was a massacre of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kurdish_people" title="wikilink">Kurdish people</a> (<a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alevism" title="wikilink">Alevi</a> <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kurmanj" title="wikilink">Kurmanj</a> and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zaza_people" title="wikilink">Zaza</a>) by the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkey" title="wikilink">Turkish government</a> in the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dersim" title="wikilink">Dersim</a> region of eastern Turkey, which includes parts of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tunceli_Province" title="wikilink">Tunceli Province</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elazığ_Province" title="wikilink">Elazığ Province</a>, and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bingöl_Province" title="wikilink">Bingöl Province</a>.[302][303][304][305][306][307][308] The massacre occurred after a rebellion led by <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Seyid_Riza" title="wikilink">Seyid Riza</a> against the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkification" title="wikilink">Turkification</a> policies of the Turkish government.[309] As a result of the Turkish military campaign against the rebellion, thousands of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alevi" title="wikilink">Alevi</a> <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zazas" title="wikilink">Zazas</a>[310] died and many others were internally displaced due to the conflict. – Part of the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kurdish_rebellions_in_Turkey" title="wikilink">Kurdish Rebellions in Turkey</a></p></td>

<tr class="even">
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_Indian_massacres" title="wikilink">Indian massacres</a> in the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" title="wikilink">United States</a> frontiers</p></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td><p>What is now the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" title="wikilink">United States</a></p></td>
<td><p>1511</p></td>
<td><p>1890</p></td>
<td><p>379 years</p></td>
<td><p>It is difficult to determine the total number of people who died as a result of Indian massacres. However, one book, <em>The Wild Frontier: Atrocities during the American-Indian War from Jamestown Colony to Wounded Knee</em>, presents an estimate by counting every recorded atrocity in the area that would eventually become the continental United States, from first contact (1511) to the closing of the frontier (1890). The parameters were limited to the intentional and indiscriminate <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/murder" title="wikilink">murder</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/torture" title="wikilink">torture</a>, or mutilation of civilians, the wounded, and prisoners. The results revealed that 7,193 people died from atrocities perpetrated by those of European descent, and 9,156 people died from atrocities perpetrated by Native Americans.[312]– Part of the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Native_American_Genocide" title="wikilink">Genocide of indigenous peoples in the Americas</a></p></td>

<td><p>Deaths of indigenous children in the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canadian_Indian_residential_school_system" title="wikilink">Canadian residential schools</a> system</p></td>

## 政治的粛清・弾圧

*This section lists events that entail the mass killings of political opposition (such as those of certain ideology, class or political persuasion).*

*See also: [Red Terror (disambiguation)](https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Red_Terror_\(disambiguation\) "wikilink"), [White Terror](https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/White_Terror_\(disambiguation\) "wikilink"), and [Politicide](https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Politicide "wikilink").*

<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mass_killings_of_landlords_under_Mao_Zedong" title="wikilink">Mass killings of landlords under Mao Zedong</a></p></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/People&#39;s_Republic_of_China" title="wikilink">People's Republic of China</a></p></td>
<td><p>1947</p></td>
<td><p>1951</p></td>
<td><p>4 years</p></td>
<td><p>Millions of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/landlords" title="wikilink">landlords</a> were killed during land reforms before the formation of the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/People&#39;s_Republic_of_China" title="wikilink">People's Republic of China</a> because they were seen as class enemies.[345]<br />
See also: <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Struggle_session" title="wikilink">Struggle session</a></p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="even">
<td><p><a href="../Page/文化大革命.md" title="wikilink">文化大革命</a></p></td>
<td><p>[346]</p></td>
<td><p>[347]</p></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/People&#39;s_Republic_of_China" title="wikilink">People's Republic of China</a></p></td>
<td><p>1966</p></td>
<td><p>1976</p></td>
<td><p>10 years</p></td>
<td><p>The <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cultural_Revolution" title="wikilink">Cultural Revolution</a>, formally the <em>Great Proletarian Cultural Revolution</em>, was a sociopolitical movement that took place in the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/People&#39;s_Republic_of_China" title="wikilink">People's Republic of China</a> from 1966 until 1976. Set into motion by <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mao_Zedong" title="wikilink">Mao Zedong</a>, then <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chairman" title="wikilink">Chairman</a> of the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Communist_Party_of_China" title="wikilink">Communist Party of China</a>, its stated goal was to preserve 'true' <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Communist_ideology" title="wikilink">Communist ideology</a> in the country by purging remnants of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/capitalist" title="wikilink">capitalist</a> and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/traditional" title="wikilink">traditional</a> elements from Chinese society.<br />
See also: <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Struggle_session" title="wikilink">Struggle session</a></p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="odd">
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indonesian_mass_killings_of_1965–66" title="wikilink">Indonesian mass killings of 1965–66</a></p></td>
<td><p>[348]</p></td>
<td><p>[349]</p></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indonesia" title="wikilink">Indonesia</a></p></td>
<td><p>1965</p></td>
<td><p>1966</p></td>
<td><p>1 year</p></td>
<td><p>Massacres of people connected to the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indonesian_Communist_Party" title="wikilink">Indonesian Communist Party</a> (PKI) were carried out in 1965–66 by the Indonesian Army and associated death squads with support from Western powers such as the United States.[350] Death tolls are difficult to estimate,[351] but it is widely accepted by scholars that roughly 1 million people were killed.[352]</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="even">
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Campaign_to_Suppress_Counterrevolutionaries_in_China" title="wikilink">Campaign to Suppress Counterrevolutionaries</a></p></td>
<td><p>[353]</p></td>
<td><p>[354]</p></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/People&#39;s_Republic_of_China" title="wikilink">People's Republic of China</a></p></td>
<td><p>1950</p></td>
<td><p>1951</p></td>
<td><p>1 year</p></td>
<td><p>The <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Campaign_to_Suppress_Counterrevolutionaries" title="wikilink">Campaign to Suppress Counterrevolutionaries</a> ( or abbreviated as ) was the first political campaign launched by the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/People&#39;s_Republic_of_China" title="wikilink">People's Republic of China</a> designed to eradicate opposition elements, especially former <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kuomintang" title="wikilink">Kuomintang</a> (KMT) functionaries accused of trying undermine the new <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Communist_Party_of_China" title="wikilink">Communist government</a>.[355]</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="odd">
<td><p><a href="../Page/大粛清.md" title="wikilink">大粛清</a></p></td>
<td><p>[356]</p></td>

The rebels killed many Ba'athist officials and officers. In response, thousands of unarmed civilians were killed by indiscriminate fire from loyalist tanks, artillery and helicopters, and many historical and religious structures in the south were deliberately targeted under orders from Saddam Hussein. Saddam's security forces entered the cities, often using women and children as <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/human_shield" title="wikilink">human shields</a>, where they detained and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/summary_execution" title="wikilink">summarily executed</a> or <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Forced_disappearance" title="wikilink">"disappeared"</a> thousands of people at random in a policy of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/collective_responsibility" title="wikilink">collective responsibility</a>. Many suspects were tortured, raped, or burned alive.[373]</p></td>

## 強制労働・奴隷貿易

*This section lists deaths caused by poor labor conditions, executions for not performing labor satisfactorily, and deaths caused by mistreatment of the workforce both in transit and at work locations.*

<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_East" title="wikilink">Middle East</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_Africa" title="wikilink">North Africa</a>, and the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Horn_of_Africa" title="wikilink">Horn of Africa</a></p></td>

<tr class="even">
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/労働改造所" title="wikilink">労働改造制度</a></p></td>
<td><p>[403]</p></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/China" title="wikilink">China</a></p></td>
<td><p>1945</p></td>
<td><p>1976</p></td>
<td><p>31 years</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Laogai" title="wikilink">Laogai</a> (勞改/劳改), the abbreviation for <em>Láodòng Gǎizào</em> (勞動改造/劳动改造), which means "reform through labor", is a slogan of the Chinese <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/criminal_justice" title="wikilink">criminal justice system</a> and has been used to refer to the use of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/penal_labour" title="wikilink">penal labour</a> and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/prison_farm" title="wikilink">prison farms</a> in the People's Republic of China (PRC), which once took up more than half of the world's slaves. <em>Laogai</em> is different from <em>laojiao</em>, or <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/re-education_through_labor" title="wikilink">re-education through labor</a>, which was an administrative detention for a person who was not a criminal but had committed minor offenses, and was intended to reform offenders into law-abiding citizens.[404] Persons detained under <em>laojiao</em> were detained in facilities that were separate from the general prison system of <em>laogai</em>. Both systems, however, involved <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Penal_labour" title="wikilink">penal labor</a>.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="odd">

<td><p>[405]</p></td>
<td><p>[406]</p></td>
<td></td>

<td><p>1450</p></td>
<td><p>1800</p></td>
<td><p>350 years</p></td>
<td><p>There is no concrete number for the number of people killed due to the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barbary_Slave_Trade" title="wikilink">Barbary Slave Trade</a>. <td></td>
<td><p>23 years</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Association_of_the_Congo" title="wikilink">Private forces</a> under the control of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leopold_II_of_Belgium" title="wikilink">Leopold II of Belgium</a> carried out mass murders, mutilations, and other crimes against the Congolese in order to encourage the gathering of valuable raw materials, principally <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/rubber" title="wikilink">rubber</a>. Significant deaths also occurred due to major disease outbreaks and starvation, caused by population displacement and poor treatment.[409] Estimates of the death toll vary considerably because of the lack of a formal census before 1924, but a commonly cited figure of 10 million deaths was obtained by estimating a 50% decline in the total population during the Congo Free State and applying it to the total population of 10 million in 1924.[410]</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="even">
<td><p><a href="../Page/グラグ.md" title="wikilink">グラグ</a>制度</p></td>
<td><p>[411][412]</p></td>

<td><p>1930s</p></td>
<td><p>1950s</p></td>
<td><p>20 years</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gulag" title="wikilink">Gulag</a> is an acronym for the organization that administered the forced labor system in the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="wikilink">Soviet Union</a> that became a colloquialism in the west for the camps themselves. The system was used to punish criminals, political dissidents, and prisoners of war. There is a growing consensus among scholars that, based on archival data, the number of deaths in the gulag system fall within the range 1.5 to 1.7 million.[414][415][416]</p></td>

Rummel</a>, coiner of the word "<a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Democide" title="wikilink">Democide</a>," estimated the mortality rate for <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mexico" title="wikilink">Mexican</a> <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peonage" title="wikilink">Peonage</a>, a form of debt labor, by comparing it to similar forced labor systems such as the Soviet <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gulag" title="wikilink">Gulag</a>, and then applying and reducing it accordingly to the population of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mexico" title="wikilink">Mexico</a> at the time, coming up with an annual death rate of 69,000.</p></td>

<td><p><a href="../Page/泰緬鉄道.md" title="wikilink">泰緬鉄道</a>の建設</p></td>
<td><p>[424]</p></td>
<td><p>[425]</p></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Burma" title="wikilink">Burma</a></p></td>
<td><p>1943</p></td>
<td><p>1947</p></td>
<td><p>4 years</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Forced_labour" title="wikilink">Forced labour</a> was used in the construction of the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Burma_Railway" title="wikilink">Burma Railway</a>. More than 180,000 Southeast Asian civilian labourers (<a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romusha" title="wikilink">Romusha</a>) and 60,000 <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Allies_of_World_War_II" title="wikilink">Allied</a> <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/prisoners_of_war" title="wikilink">prisoners of war</a> (POWs) worked on the railway. Of these, estimates of Romusha deaths are little more than guesses, but probably about 90,000 died. 12,621 Allied POWs died during the construction. The dead POWs included 6,904 <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_people" title="wikilink">British</a> personnel, 2,802 <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australians" title="wikilink">Australians</a>, 2,782 <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_people" title="wikilink">Dutch</a>, and 133 <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Americans" title="wikilink">Americans</a>.[426]</p></td>

<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Egypt" title="wikilink">Egypt</a>, and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sudan" title="wikilink">Sudan</a></p></td>

<td><p>9 years</p></td>
<td><p>French diplomat <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ferdinand_de_Lesseps" title="wikilink">Ferdinand de Lesseps</a> had obtained many concessions from <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isma&#39;il_Pasha" title="wikilink">Isma'il Pasha</a>, the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Khedive" title="wikilink">Khedive</a> of Egypt and Sudan in 1854–56 to build the Suez Canal. Some sources estimate the workforce at 30,000,[427] but others estimate that 120,000 workers died over the ten years of construction due to malnutrition, fatigue, and disease, especially <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/cholera" title="wikilink">cholera</a>.[428]</p></td>

<tr class="even">
<td><p>ペルーにおける中国人労働者の強制労働</p></td>
<td><p>[429]</p></td>
<td><p>[430]</p></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peru" title="wikilink">Peru</a></p></td>
<td><p>1849</p></td>
<td><p>1874</p></td>
<td><p>26 years</p></td>
<td><p>80,000[431] to 100,000[432][433] Chinese contract laborers, 95% of which were Cantonese and almost all of which were male, were sent mostly to the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/sugar" title="wikilink">sugar</a> plantations from 1849 to 1874, during the termination of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/slavery" title="wikilink">slavery</a>. They were to provide continuous labor for the coastal <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/guano" title="wikilink">guano</a> mines and especially for the coastal plantations where they became a major labor force (contributing greatly to the Peruvian <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Guano_Era" title="wikilink">guano boom</a>) until the end of the century. While the coolies were believed to be reduced to virtual slaves, they also represented a historical transition from slave to free labor. A third group of Chinese workers was contracted for the construction of the railway from Lima to <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/La_Oroya" title="wikilink">La Oroya</a> and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Huancayo" title="wikilink">Huancayo</a>. Chinese migrants were barred from using cemeteries reserved for Roman Catholics, and were instead buried at pre-Incan burial sites.[434] Between 1849 and 1874 half[435][436] the Chinese population of Peru perished due to abuse, exhaustion, and suicide[437] caused by forced labor.[438][439]</p></td>
</tr>

<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_famine_of_1917–1919" title="wikilink">Iranian famine of 1917–1919</a></p></td>
<td><p>[460][461]</p></td>

<td></td>
<td><p>Iran</p></td>
<td><p>1917</p></td>
<td><p>1919</p></td>
<td><p>3 years</p></td>
<td><p>The Persian famine of 1917–1919 was a period of widespread mass starvation and disease in <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iran" title="wikilink">Persia (Iran)</a>. The famine took place in the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_Campaign" title="wikilink">occupied territory</a> of Iran that had declared neutrality. According to the estimates acknowledged, 2–10 million people died of hunger and disease. A variety of factors are commented to have caused and contributed to the famine such as war profiteering, and poor harvests but mainly requisitioning and confiscation of foodstuffs by the occupying Russian and British armies.[464][465]</p></td>
</tr>

Economic mismanagement and the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_Korea–Russia_relations#1985–1991" title="wikilink">loss of Soviet support</a> caused food production and imports to decline rapidly. A series of floods and droughts exacerbated the crisis, but were not its direct cause. The <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Politics_of_North_Korea" title="wikilink">North Korean government</a> and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Economy_of_North_Korea" title="wikilink">its centrally-planned system</a> proved too inflexible to effectively curtail the disaster. Recent research suggests the likely number of excess deaths between 1993 and 2000 was about 330,000.[492][493]</p></td>

## 人為的に悪化させられた洪水・地すべり

*These are floods and landslides that have been partially caused by humans, for example by failure of [dam](https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/dam "wikilink")s, [levee](https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/levee "wikilink")s, [seawall](https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/seawall "wikilink")s or [retaining walls](https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/retaining_wall "wikilink").*

<td><p>1946</p></td>
<td><p>1976</p></td>
<td><p>30 years</p></td>
<td><p>Critics of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mao_Zedong" title="wikilink">Mao Zedong</a> have argued <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mao_Zedong" title="wikilink">Mao</a>'s China saw unprecedented losses of human life through inhuman economic policies such as the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Leap_Forward" title="wikilink">Great Leap Forward</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Laogai" title="wikilink">slave labor through the Laogai</a>, violent political purges such as the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cultural_Revolution" title="wikilink">Cultural Revolution</a> the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Campaign_to_Suppress_Counterrevolutionaries" title="wikilink">Campaign to Suppress Counterrevolutionaries</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Land_reform_in_China" title="wikilink">and class extermination through land reform</a> The estimate of the minimum death toll is the sum of the minimum estimate of famine dead (11.6 million),[556] land reform dead (800,000),[557] Counterrevolutionaries dead (712,000),[558] and Cultural Revolution dead (400,000)[559] plus the minimum killed in the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/1959_Tibetan_uprising" title="wikilink">1959 Tibetan uprising</a> (85,000 to 87,000) </p></td>

<td><p>11 years</p></td>

<li>4,900,000 to 6,200,000 Jews killed (2/3s to 78% of European Jewry killed)[563][564][565]</li>

<li>2,470,000<ref>Zemskov, Viktor N. (2012). "О масштабах людских потерь CCCР в Великой Отечественной Войне" [The extent of human losses USSR in the Great Patriotic War]. Military Historical Archive (Военно-исторический архив) (in Russian). 9: 59–71 – via Demoskop Weehly vol. 559–560 (2013)<br />
Excludes:</li>
</ul></li>
<li>Excludes the 2,500,000 million Jewish civilians killed in Soviet Territories-(see: Gilbert, Martin. Atlas of the Holocaust. 1988. )</li>
<li>30,000 to 35,000 Roma killed in Porajmos-(see: Niewyk, Donald L. (2000). The Columbia Guide to the Holocaust. Columbia University Press. p. 422. . "European Romani (Gypsy) Population". The United States Holocaust Memorial Museum: Holocaust Encyclopedia. Retrieved January 8, 2016..</ref> to 11,149,692<ref></li>
</ul>
<p>Includes:</p>
<ul>
<li>Deaths caused by the result of direct, intentional actions of violence 7,420,379-(see: ????????? 1995, pp. 124–131 The Russian Academy of Science article by M.V. Philimoshin based this figure on sources published in the Soviet era.)</li>
<li>Deaths of forced laborers in Germany 2,164,313-(see: Евдокимов 1995, pp. 124–131.)</li>
<li>Deaths due to famine and disease in the occupied regions 4,100,000-(see: Евдокимов 1995, pp. 124–131 The Russian Academy of Science article by M.V. Philimoshin estimated 6% of the population in the occupied regions died due to war related famine and disease.)</li>
</ul>
<p>Excludes:</p>
<ul>
<li>Excludes the 2,500,000 million Jewish civilians killed in Soviet Territories-(see: Gilbert, Martin. Atlas of the Holocaust. 1988. )</li>
<li>30,000 to 35,000 Roma killed in Porajmos-(see: Niewyk, Donald L. (2000). The Columbia Guide to the Holocaust. Columbia University Press. p. 422. . "European Romani (Gypsy) Population". The United States Holocaust Memorial Museum: Holocaust Encyclopedia. <li><ul>

</ul></li>
<li>3,135,000 to 3,325,000 <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_mistreatment_of_Soviet_prisoners_of_war" title="wikilink">Non-Jewish Soviet POWs killed by Nazis</a><ref></li>
</ul></li>

<p></ref></p>
<ul>
<li><ul>
<li>1,800,000<ref></li>
</ul></li>
</ul>
<p></ref> to 2,770,000[567] <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nazi_crimes_against_the_Polish_nation" title="wikilink">Poles and other Non-Jews killed by Nazis in Poland</a></p>
<ul>
<li>130,000[568] to 500,000[569] killed in <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Porajmos" title="wikilink">Porajmos</a> (1/4 of Roma population)</li>
<li>300,000 to 600,000 <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/World_War_II_persecution_of_Serbs" title="wikilink">Serbians killed</a> by the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ustaše" title="wikilink">Ustaše</a>[570]</li>

<li>77,000 members of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_resistance_to_Nazism" title="wikilink">German resistance against Nazism executed</a>[575]</li>
<li>20,000 to 25,000 Slovenes<ref>The number of Slovenes estimated to have died as a result of the Nazi occupation (not including those killed by Slovene collaboration forces and other Nazi allies) is estimated between 20,000 and 25,000 people. This number only includes civilians: Slovene partisan POWs who died and resistance fighters killed in action are not included (their number is estimated at 27,000). These numbers however include only Slovenes from present-day Slovenia: it does not include Carinthian Slovene victims, nor Slovene victims from areas in present-day Italy and Croatia. These numbers are result of a 10-year-long research by the Institute for Contemporary History (Inštitut za novejšo zgodovino) from Ljubljana, Slovenia. The partial results of the research have been released in 2008 in the volume Žrtve vojne in revolucije v Sloveniji (Ljubljana: Institute for Contemporary History, 2008), and officially presented at the Slovenian National Council</li>
</ul>
<p><a href="http://www.ds-rs.si/sites/default/files/dokumenti/zbornik_zrtve_vojne_in_revolucije.pdf">http://www.ds-rs.si/sites/default/files/dokumenti/zbornik_zrtve_vojne_in_revolucije.pdf</a></ref></p>
<ul>
<li>18,000[576] to 22,000[577] <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_famine_of_1944–45" title="wikilink">Dutch famine of 1944–45</a></li>
<li>7,000 Spanish Republican killed[578]</li>
<li>5,000 to 15,000 <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_homosexuals_in_Nazi_Germany_and_the_Holocaust" title="wikilink">Homosexuals killed</a>[579]</li>

</ul></td>

<tr class="odd">
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Stalin" title="wikilink">Joseph Stalin</a></p></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="wikilink">Soviet Union</a></p></td>
<td><p>1922</p></td>
<td><p>1953</p></td>
<td><p>31 years</p></td>
<td><p>The millions killed by the regime of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Stalin" title="wikilink">Joseph Stalin</a> through <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soviet_famine_of_1932-33" title="wikilink">famine</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Purge" title="wikilink">purges</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gulag" title="wikilink">labor camps</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Population_transfer_in_the_Soviet_Union" title="wikilink">population transfer</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Deportation_of_the_Crimean_Tatars" title="wikilink">deportations</a>, and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_Operation_of_the_NKVD_(1937–38)" title="wikilink">NKVD massacres.</a> The minimum death toll (to the left) uses the minimum post-archive calculations from after the fall of the Soviet regime of those not killed in famine which range from four to ten million[583][584][585] <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Conquest" title="wikilink">Robert Conquest</a>, writer of the book <em><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Great_Terror" title="wikilink">The Great Terror</a></em>, first stated an estimate of 30 million, then a few years later lowering it to 20 million,[586] and finally saying that no fewer than 15 million perished during the entire history of the USSR.[587] Following the collapse of the USSR and the opening of the archives, scholars have reached lower death tolls.[588]</p>
<p>The minimum death toll (to the left) uses the minimum post-archive calculations from after the fall of the Soviet regime of those not killed in famine[589]</p>
<p>Timothy D. Snyder in 2011 said that Stalin approximately killed 6 million to 9 million [590]</p>

<tr class="odd">
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leopold_II_of_Belgium" title="wikilink">Leopold II of Belgium</a></p></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Congo_Free_State" title="wikilink">Congo Free State</a></p></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td><p>13 years</p></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Association_of_the_Congo" title="wikilink">Private forces</a> under the control of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leopold_II_of_Belgium" title="wikilink">Leopold II of Belgium</a> carried out mass murders, mutilations, and other crimes against the Congolese in order to encourage the gathering of valuable raw materials, principally <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/rubber" title="wikilink">rubber</a>. Significant deaths also occurred due to major disease outbreaks and starvation, caused by population displacement and poor treatment.[593] Estimates of the death toll vary considerably due to the lack of a formal census before 1924, but a commonly cited figure of 10 million deaths was obtained by estimating a 50% decline in the total population during the Congo Free State and applying it to the total population of 10 million in 1924.[594] See also: <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Atrocities_in_the_Congo_Free_State" title="wikilink">Atrocities in the Congo Free State</a></p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="even">
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ranavalona_I" title="wikilink">Ranavalona I</a></p></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Madagascar" title="wikilink">Madagascar</a></p></td>
<td><p>1829</p></td>
<td><p>1842</p></td>
<td><p>13 years</p></td>
<td><p>Putting an end to most foreign trade relationships, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ranavalona_I" title="wikilink">Ranavalona I</a> pursued a policy of self-reliance, made possible through frequent use of the long-standing tradition of <em><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Corvée#Madagascar" title="wikilink">fanompoana</a></em>—forced labor in lieu of tax payments in money or goods. Ranavalona continued the wars of expansion conducted by her predecessor, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Radama_I" title="wikilink">Radama I</a>, in an effort to extend her realm over the entire island, and imposed strict punishments on those who were judged as having acted in opposition to her will. Due in large part to loss of life throughout the years of military campaigns, high death rates among <em>fanompoana</em> workers, and harsh traditions of justice under her rule, the population of Madagascar is estimated to have declined from around 5 million to 2.5 million between 1833–39, and from 750,000 to 130,000 between 1829–42 in Imerina.[595] These statistics have contributed to a strongly unfavorable view of Ranavalona's rule in historical accounts.[596]</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="odd">
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pol_Pot" title="wikilink">Pol Pot</a></p></td>
<td><p>[597]</p></td>
<td><p>[598]</p></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Democratic_Kampuchea" title="wikilink">Cambodia</a></p></td>
<td><p>1975</p></td>
<td><p>1979</p></td>
<td><p>4 years</p></td>
<td><p>Deaths due to arbitrary torture, execution, starvation, and forced labor among the population of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cambodia" title="wikilink">Cambodia</a> under the rule of <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pol_Pot" title="wikilink">Pol Pot</a> and the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Khmer_Rouge" title="wikilink">Khmer Rouge</a>, including both killings of ethnic <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Khmer_people" title="wikilink">Khmer</a> (the majority ethnic group) as well as a <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cambodian_genocide#Ethnic_and_Religious_Victims" title="wikilink">genocide of religious and ethnic minorities by the Khmer Rouge</a>. Minimum death toll is the number of corpses found in the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Killing_Fields" title="wikilink">Killing Fields</a>.See also: <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cambodian_genocide" title="wikilink">Cambodian genocide</a></p></td>

<tr class="even">
<td><p>The <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Young_Turks" title="wikilink">Young Turks</a></p></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td><p><a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="wikilink">Ottoman Empire</a></p></td>
<td><p>1913</p></td>
<td><p>1922</p></td>
<td><p>9 years</p></td>
<td><p>Under the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Young_Turks" title="wikilink">Young Turks</a>' regime that took powerin 1908, the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="wikilink">Ottoman Empire</a> committed various <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/genocides" title="wikilink">genocides</a> and <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/ethnic_cleansings" title="wikilink">ethnic cleansings</a>. The death toll is derived from the sum of the death tolls of the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Armenian_Genocide" title="wikilink">Armenian Genocide</a> (800,000 to 1,500,000), <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Assyrian_Genocide" title="wikilink">Assyrian Genocide</a> (150,000 to 300,000), <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_Genocide" title="wikilink">Greek Genocide</a> (289,000 to 750,000), <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/ethnic_cleansing" title="wikilink">ethnic cleansing</a> of the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thracian_Bulgarians" title="wikilink">Thracian Bulgarians</a> in 1913 (50,000 to 60,000), and the <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Famine_of_Mount_Lebanon" title="wikilink">Great Famine of Mount Lebanon</a> (200,000).</p></td>

     <https://www.hawaii.edu/powerkills/SOD.TAB14.1C.GIF> row 1313 and 1314
     1,000,000 and 10,000 to 2,000,000 and 100,000 Kurds were displaced and killed respectively between 1963 and 1987; 250,000 of them in 1977 and 1978. If deaths are proportional to the displacement then 2,500 to 12,500 Kurds would of died during this period depending on the scale of overall displacement and deaths used.

214. 1,000 deaths per day in April, May and June along Turkish border *a -* "Iraqi Deaths from the Gulf War as of April 1992," Greenpeace, Washington, D.C. See also "Aftermath of War: The Persian Gulf War Refugee Crisis," Staff Report to the Senate Judiciary Committee's Subcommittee on Immigration and Refugee Affairs, May 20, 1991. The figure of nearly 1,000 deaths per day is also given in "Kurdistan in the Time of Saddam Hussein," Staff Report to the U.S. Senate Committee on Foreign Relations, November 1991, p.14. "hundreds" (100 to 900?) died per day along Iranian border *b -* [Kurdish Refugees Straggle Into Iran, Followed By Tragedy](http://www.apnewsarchive.com/1991/Kurdish-Refugees-Straggle-Into-Iran-Followed-By-Tragedy/id-2a413a508ec5af132b9cc245172f3f9c), Associated Press, Apr 13, 1991 1,100 to 1,900 (''a '' + *b*) deaths per day from at least April 13th (*b*) up to between May 1st and May 31st (''a ''); which suggests 44 to 74 days: 1,100(44)= 48,400 1,900(74)= 140,600 **Routine calculations** *Routine calculations do not count as original research, provided there is consensus among editors that the result of the calculation is obvious, correct, and a meaningful reflection of the sources. Basic arithmetic, such as adding numbers, converting units, or calculating a person's age are some examples of routine calculations. See also Category:Conversion templates.*

397. Ronald Segal, in Islam's Black Slaves, estimates the total number of African slaves shipped to the Muslim world at 11.5M-14M. This breaks down as follows: From 650-1600 CE Citing Ralph Austen: Trans-Saharan: 4,820,000 Red Sea: 1.6M East Africa: 0.8M TOTAL: 7.22M shipped Citing Paul Lovejoy: 3.5-10.0M shipped 17th Century Sahara: 0.7M Red Sea: 0.1M East Africa: 0.1M TOTAL: 900,000 shipped 18th C Sahara: 0.7M Red Sea: 0.2M East Africa: 0.4M TOTAL: 1,300,000 shipped 19th C Sahara: 1.2M Red Sea: 0.45M East Africa: 0.442M TOTAL: 2,092,000 shipped TOTAL: 11,512,000 shipped Segal also mentions estimates by Raymond Mauvy: 7th C: 0.1M 8th C: 0.2M 9th C: 0.4M 10th-13th Cs: 2.0M 14th C: 1.0M 15th-19th Cs: 10.0M First half 20th C.: 300,000 TOTAL: 14M shipped What was the mortality rate among these slaves? Here are a few estimates in Segal: Wylde: Each eunuch in Cairo represented 200 dead Sudanese. Hourst, 19th C: each sale represented a loss of ten in the original population, including raids. Livingstone: 1 living = 10 dead. British Govt Rpt: For every 10 slaves reaching 19C Cairo, 50 died on the way. Nachtigal: on one large \[typical?\] Saharan caravan, 3 or 4 died for every survivor. UK Consul in Zanzibar: 1:1 ratio Mahadi: 20% d. in Saharan trade Lovejoy, citing Martin: 9% overall in 19th C. East Africa. (Segal: safe estimate) \[MEDIAN of these estimates: 3 to 5 deaths for every 1 live import\]

460. Katouzian 2013, p. 1934: "Russian Revolution of 1917 brought much relief to Iran after a century of imperial interference and intimidation. But it was followed by severe famine and the Spanish flu pandemic which, combined, took a high toll of around two million, mostly of the Iranian poor."
461. Rubin 2015, p. 508: "Despite Iran's official neutrality, this pattern of interference continued during World War I as Ottoman-, Russian-, British-, and German-supported local forces fought across Iran, wreaking enormous havoc on the country. With farmland, crops, livestock, and infrastructure destroyed, as many as 2 million Iranians died of famine at the war's end. Although the Russian Revolution of 1917 led to the recall of Russian troops, and thus gave hope to Iranians that the foreign yoke might be relenting, the British quickly moved to fill the vacuum in the north, and by 1918, had turned the country into an unofficial protectorate."
462. [Winegard 2016](https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_famine_of_1917–1919#CITEREFWinegard2016 "wikilink"), p. 85: "Between 1917 and 1919, it is estimated that nearly half (nine to eleven million people) of the Persian population died of starvation or disease brought on by malnutrition."

522. This toll is only for the number of Japanese pilots killed in Kamikaze suicide missions. 563. Reitlinger, Gerald (1953). The Final Solution. The Attempt to Exterminate the Jews of Europe, 1939–1945. New York City: Beechhurst Press.
564. Early efforts by scholars to determine the number of Jews murdered by the Nazis were limited by a lack of access to pertinent records. The genocide seldom entered Western discourse, both due to ignorance and to the Cold-War politics which made West Germany a new ally of the United States.The first significant work on the subject published in English was Gerald Reitlinger's Final Solution (1953), which, relying almost exclusively on German documentation, estimated 4.9 million dead. This figure is now considered extremely conservative. Raul Hilberg's 1961 [The Destruction of the European Jews](https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Destruction_of_the_European_Jews "wikilink") became a classic in the field of Holocaust literature and made the genocide of the Jews known to the wider public, Hilberg estimated its victims to be 5.1 million lives, or 4.9 – 5.4 million broadly construed. The trial of Adolph Eichmann further raised awareness of the genocide, Eichmann also provided documentation and testimony which revised the number of the dead.The first work to arrive at a figure comparable to modern estimates was Lucy Dawidowicz's The War Against the Jews, published in 1975, the book provided detailed listings by country of the number of Jews killed in the Holocaust which are still used as a reference in modern Holocaust studies. Dawidowicz researched birth and death records in many cities of prewar Europe to come up with a death toll of 5,933,900 Jews. After the opening of Soviet records, scholarship arrived at a death toll of about 6 million Jews. Gutman and Rozett's Encyclopedia of the Holocaust was published in 1990 and estimated slightly over 5.9 million Jews were murdered.Wolfgang Benz's The Holocaust: A German Historian Examines the Genocide, published 1995, gave a toll of 6.2 million.
565. Davies, Norman (2012). God's Playground \[Boze igrzysko\]. Otwarte (publishing). p. 956. . Polish edition, second volume. "To, co robili Sowieci, bylo szczególnie mylace. Same liczby bylSacramentsie wiarygodne, ale pozbawione komentarza, sprytnie ukrywaly fakt, ze ofiary w przewazajacej liczbie nie byly Rosjanami, ze owe miliony obejmowaly ofiary nie tylko Hitlera, ale i Stalina, oraz ze wsród ludnosci cywilnej najwieksze grupy stanowili Ukraincy, Polacy, Bialorusini i Zydzi. Translation: The Soviet methods were particularly misleading. The numbers were correct, but the victims were overwhelmingly not Russian, and came from either one of the two regimes."

Human Losses and Victims of Repression under two Occupations\]. Warsaw: Institute of National Remembrance (IPN). Archived from the original on March 23, 2012. – Janusz Kurtyka; Zbigniew Gluza. Preface.: "ze pod okupacja sowiecka zginelo w latach 1939–1941, a nastepnie 1944–1945 co najmniej 150 tys \[...\] Laczne straty smiertelne ludnosci polskiej pod okupacja niemiecka oblicza sie obecnie na ok. 2 770 000. \[...\] Do tych strat nalezy doliczyc ponad 100 tys. Polaków pomordowanych w latach 1942–1945 przez nacjonalistów ukrainskich (w tym na samym Wolyniu ok. 60 tys. osób \[...\] Liczba Zydów i Polaków zydowskiego pochodzenia, obywateli II Rzeczypospolitej, zamordowanych przez Niemców siega 2,7– 2,9 mln osób." Translation: "It must be assumed losses of at least 150.000 people during the Soviet occupation from 1939 to 1941 and again from 1944 to 1945 \[...\] The total fatalities of the Polish population under the German occupation are now estimated at 2,770,000. \[...\] To these losses should be added more than 100,000 Poles murdered in the years 1942–1945 by Ukrainian nationalists (including about 60,000 in Volhynia \[...\] The number of Jews and Poles of Jewish ethnicity, citizens of the Second Polish Republic, murdered by the Germans amounts to 2.7–2.9 million people." – Waldemar Grabowski. German and Soviet occupation. Fundamental issues.: "Straty ludnosci panstwa polskiego narodowosci ukrainskiej sa trudne do wyliczenia," Translation: "The losses of ethnic Poles of Ukrainian nationality are difficult to calculate." Note: Polish losses amount to 11.3% of the 24.4 million ethnic Poles in prewar Poland and about 90 percent of the 3.3 million Jews of prewar times. The IPN figures do not include losses among Polish citizens of Ukrainian and Belarusian ethnicity. <https://web.archive.org/web/20120323161233/http://niniwa2.cba.pl/polska_1939_1945.htm>

White 2011, pp. 455–456: "For those who prefer totals broken down by country, here are reasonable estimates for the number of people who died under Communist regimes from execution, labor camps, famine, ethnic cleansing, and desperate flight in leaky boats: China: 40,000,000 Soviet Union: 20,000,000 North Korea: 3,000,000 Ethiopia: 2,000,000 Cambodia: 1,700,000 Vietnam: 365,000 (after 1975) Yugoslavia: 175,000 East Germany: 100,000 Romania: 100,000 North Vietnam: 50,000 (internally, 1954–75) Cuba: 50,000 Mongolia: 35,000 Poland: 30,000 Bulgaria: 20,000 Czechoslovakia: 11,000 Albania: 5,000 Hungary: 5,000 Rough Total: 70 million (This rough total doesn't include the 20 million killed in the civil wars that brought Communists into power, or the 11 million who died in the proxy wars of the Cold War. Both sides probably share the blame for these to a certain extent. These two categories overlap somewhat, so once the duplicates are weeded out, it seems that some 26 million people died in Communist-inspired wars.)"

Noting that the [Iran–Iraq War](https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iran–Iraq_War "wikilink") cost approximately 800,000 lives on both sides and that—while "surely a gross exaggeration"—Iraq estimated there were 100,000 deaths resulting from U.S. bombing in the [Gulf War](https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gulf_War "wikilink"), Burns concludes: "A million dead Iraqis, in war and through terror, may not be far from the mark."
